GPU Boost 3.0: Finer-Grained Clockspeed Controls

07 Sep 2024, 00:00

While much of this is abstracted away in everyday GPU discussions, under the hood the concept of clockspeed is a little lot more complex than the simple base clock and boost clock numbers posted in specification tables. Since the introduction of Kepler, NVIDIA has introduced fine-grained voltage points, which defines a series of GPU voltages and their respective clockspeeds. The GPU in turn operates at points along the resulting curve, shifting clockspeeds based on which voltage it‚Äôs at and what the environmental conditions are.

What are Strepsirhines and Haplorhines?

02 Sep 2024, 00:00

The lower primates or strepsirhines (suborder Strepsirhini) include lemurs, bush babies, lorises; the higher primates or haplorhines (suborder Haplorhini) include the tarsiers, Old and New World monkeys, apes and humans. Strepsirhines have moist noses; haplorhines have simple, dry noses.Click to see full answer. Why does Tennessee have the Oilers logo?

02 Aug 2024, 00:00

Tennessee has the Oilers logo because the Tennessee Titans, the state‚Äôs NFL team, has a historical connection to the Houston Oilers. The Houston Oilers were a member of the AFL and then the NFL from 1960 to 1996. Owned by Bud Adams, the team had unique Columbia blue uniforms and a derrick logo that stood out as a unique brand during their time in Houston. In 1997, Adams relocated the team from Houston to Tennessee, where they were known as the Tennessee Oilers for two years before ultimately becoming the Tennessee Titans.

Do blondes go bald faster?

21 Jul 2024, 00:00

While you may have heard that blonds suffer more hair loss than brunettes, the reality is that your natural hair color doesn't have any effect on your likelihood of experiencing hair loss. Do you lose hair when you go blonde? DraelosHair dyeing does not inhibit hair growth, but it may cause hair loss by damaging the hair that is color treated. Hair beneath the scalp that has not yet emerged cannot be reached by hair dye and thus hair dye cannot fundamentally cause hair loss, but hair shedding can increase with hair dyeing.

Random Read/Write Speed The four corners of SSD performance are as follows: random read, random write, sequential read and sequential write speed. Our first test writes 4KB in a completely random pattern over an 8GB space of the drive to simulate the sort of random access that you'd see on an OS drive (even this is more stressful than a normal desktop user would see).

Sweet William (Dianthus barbutus) is a perennial flower that is widely planted as an annual or biennial. Deadheading sweet Williams after each bloom lengthens the plant life and blooming season. What does it mean if KEQ equals 1?

31 May 2024, 00:00

Answer Keq = 1, which indicates that the location of equilibrium is in the middle, and that the number of products at equilibrium is about equal to the amount of reactants. If Keq is a small number (for example, if Keq = 10-3), then the location of equilibrium is to the left, indicating that there are more reactants present at equilibrium than at the starting point. What does KEQ stand for, then, in light of all of this?
